This optimization is based on various factors, including technician performance (sales, flip rate), location (minimizing drive time), and job type. The software aims to increase revenue by sending the \\\"right tech to the right call\\\" and improve operational efficiency by streamlining the dispatch process.\\n\\nProbook offers two main product tiers:\\n1.  **Copilot:** This level provides AI-powered recommendations for dispatching. It assists dispatchers in making decisions by suggesting the best technician for a job at the click of a button. It includes real-time syncing with ServiceTitan and keeps dispatchers informed with recommendations.\\n2.  **Autopilot:** This is a higher level of automation where the software fully reshuffles the dispatch board in real-time. Dispatchers verify job parameters to ensure accuracy, and this level is designed to allow a single dispatcher to manage a larger number of technicians (20-25+).\\n\\nProbook's services include the software itself, a 2-day in-person launch with their CEO for onboarding and support, and ongoing customer service with fast response and resolution times. They position themselves as the \\\"premiere AI dispatching solution\\\" built by dispatchers for dispatchers, emphasizing ease of use, trust in decisions, and continuous feature development. They highlight their ability to drive significant growth in average ticket size, flip rate, and technician-to-dispatcher ratio.\\n\\nProbook provides unparalleled visibility through various dashboards and features:\\n-   **Tech Performance:** Blends repair and TGL (Turned-in Generated Lead) sales into an average per call type, identifies training opportunities, and weighs recent data more heavily to capture short-term trends.\\n-   **Tech Speed:** Forecasts how long techs will take at each call using historical data, identifies techs who need to slow down, and shows accurate job lengths on the dispatch board.\\n-   **Geography:** Shows average revenue and job count by zip code to identify marketing opportunities and how specific job types perform in different zip codes.\\n-   **7 Day Call Board:** Integrates with ServiceTitan in real-time, allows setting thresholds for specific trades, job types, and tag bundles, and automatically shows when thresholds are near or above.\\n\\nProbook's market positioning is focused on helping home service companies move beyond manual or \\\"gut feeling\\\" based dispatching to a data-driven, optimized approach that directly impacts their bottom line and operational efficiency. They target companies looking to increase sales, improve technician productivity, reduce drive time, enhance dispatcher efficiency, and provide better customer service.\\n\\nClearly identified This is important to ensure the code remains valid and functional, and the users see a working website preview.\\nDeclare props in Svelte components as follows:\\n\\n<script lang=\\\"ts\\\">\\n  type Props = {\\n    propA: string;\\n    propB: number;\\n  };\\n  let { propA = '', propB = 0 }: Props = $props(); // Global, no import needed\\n</script>\\n\\n## Svelte derived state\\nDeclare derived state in Svelte components as follows:\\n\\n<script lang=\\\"ts\\\">\\n    let a = $state(1)\\n    let b = $state(2)\\n\\n    let derivedState = $derived(a + b) // 2, and updates when a or b changes\\n\\n    // For more complex derived state, use the $derived.vby function with a callback\\n    let complexDerivedState = $derived.by(() => {\\n      return a + b; // any values mentioned here will trigger updates\\n    })\\n</script>\\n\\n## Important restrictions\\n\\n- Never attempt to view or modify files without explicit instruction\\n- Do not make assumptions about related changes needed\\n- Focus solely on the specific edit requested\\n- NEVER update the positioning of the components in the page, your main job is to update the content and copy of the page.\\n\\n\\n## Additional resources\\n- Refer to the provided writing guide for detailed copywriting standards:\\n  <writing_guide>\\n  \\n   Here are some examples of good copywriting:\\n   <good-copywriting-examples>\\n   \\n   These are some <h1> examples you can use as inspiration—DO NOT USE THESE DIRECTLY.\\n   <h1-examples>\\n   - Time is money.
